<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Peer Gynt Suite No.2
</td></tr>
<tr>

<td class="wi_head">

<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Grieg,_Edvard" title="Category:Grieg, Edvard">Grieg, Edvard</a>
</td></tr>

<td>Op.55
</td></tr>

<td>IEG 78
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 pieces
<ol><li> Bruderovet, Ingrids klage (The Abduction of the Bride, Ingrid's Lament)
</li><li> Arabisk dans (Arabian Dance)
</li><li> Peer Gynts hjemfart, Stormfull aften på havet<br />(Peer Gynt's Homecoming, Stormy Evening on the Sea)
</li><li> Solveigs sang (Solveig's Song)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
